# Task: Implement COPY FROM CSV WITH HEADER MATCH for PostgreSQL

## Objective
Add a `HEADER MATCH` option to PostgreSQL's `COPY FROM` command that validates the CSV file's header row column names match the target table's column names (in order and spelling). Currently `COPY ... WITH (HEADER)` simply skips the first row; `HEADER MATCH` should verify it matches.

## Requirements

1. **Extend the COPY grammar** (`src/backend/parser/gram.y`):
   - Add `MATCH` as a valid keyword after `HEADER` in COPY options
   - The option should be: `HEADER MATCH` (two tokens) as an alternative to `HEADER` / `HEADER TRUE`
   - Store the distinction in the CopyStmt or DefElem representation

2. **Update COPY option processing** (`src/backend/commands/copy.c` or `src/backend/commands/copyfrom.c`):
   - Parse the `HEADER MATCH` option and set a flag (e.g., `header_line` enum: OFF, ON, MATCH)
   - Only valid for CSV format with COPY FROM (not COPY TO)
   - Raise an error if HEADER MATCH is used with non-CSV format or COPY TO

3. **Implement header validation** in the COPY FROM reader:
   - After reading the first line of the CSV file, compare each column name to the corresponding column in the target table's column list
   - Column comparison should be case-insensitive
   - If extra/missing/mismatched columns are found, raise an ERROR with a descriptive message listing the mismatched column names

4. **Add a regression test** in `src/test/regress/sql/copy.sql` (or a new file):
   - Test HEADER MATCH with matching headers (should succeed)
   - Test HEADER MATCH with mismatched headers (should fail with appropriate error)
   - Test HEADER MATCH with wrong column count (should fail)

## Key Reference Files
- `src/backend/parser/gram.y` — SQL grammar (search for `copy_opt_list` and `HEADER`)
- `src/backend/commands/copy.c` — COPY command entry point, option processing
- `src/backend/commands/copyfrom.c` — COPY FROM implementation
- `src/include/commands/copy.h` — CopyHeaderChoice enum and CopyFormatOptions
- `src/include/parser/kwlist.h` — keyword list (MATCH may need adding)
- `src/test/regress/sql/copy.sql` — existing COPY regression tests

## Success Criteria
- HEADER MATCH syntax accepted in SQL grammar
- CopyHeaderChoice enum or equivalent extended with MATCH value
- Header validation logic reads CSV header and compares to table columns
- Appropriate error raised on mismatch
- Regression test file exists with match/mismatch test cases

/*-------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 * copy.h
 *	  Definitions for using the POSTGRES copy command.
 *
 *
 * Portions Copyright (c) 1996-2026, PostgreSQL Global Development Group
 * Portions Copyright (c) 1994, Regents of the University of California
 *
 * src/include/commands/copy.h
 *
 *-------------------------------------------------------------------------
 */
#ifndef COPY_H
#define COPY_H

#include "nodes/execnodes.h"
#include "nodes/parsenodes.h"
#include "parser/parse_node.h"
#include "tcop/dest.h"

/*
 * Represents whether a header line must match the actual names
 * (which implies "true"), and whether it should be present.
 */
#define COPY_HEADER_MATCH	-1
#define COPY_HEADER_FALSE	0
#define COPY_HEADER_TRUE	1

/*
 * Represents where to save input processing errors.  More values to be added
 * in the future.
 */
typedef enum CopyOnErrorChoice
{
	COPY_ON_ERROR_STOP = 0,		/* immediately throw errors, default */
	COPY_ON_ERROR_IGNORE,		/* ignore errors */
	COPY_ON_ERROR_SET_NULL,		/* set error field to null */
} CopyOnErrorChoice;

+

+	style	text,
+	test 	text,
+	filler	int);
+
+insert into copytest values('DOS',E'abc\r\ndef',1);
+insert into copytest values('Unix',E'abc\ndef',2);
+insert into copytest values('Mac',E'abc\rdef',3);
+insert into copytest values(E'esc\\ape',E'a\\r\\\r\\\n\\nb',4);
+
+\set filename :abs_builddir '/results/copytest.csv'
+copy copytest to :'filename' csv;
+
+create temp table copytest2 (like copytest);
+
+copy copytest2 from :'filename' csv;
+
+select * from copytest except select * from copytest2;
+
+truncate copytest2;
+

+
+copy copytest to :'filename' csv quote '''' escape E'\\';
+
+copy copytest2 from :'filename' csv quote '''' escape E'\\';
+
+select * from copytest except select * from copytest2;
+

/*-------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 * copy.h
 *	  Definitions for using the POSTGRES copy command.
 *
 *
 * Portions Copyright (c) 1996-2021, PostgreSQL Global Development Group
 * Portions Copyright (c) 1994, Regents of the University of California
 *
 * src/include/commands/copy.h
 *
 *-------------------------------------------------------------------------
 */
#ifndef COPY_H
#define COPY_H

#include "nodes/execnodes.h"
#include "nodes/parsenodes.h"
#include "parser/parse_node.h"
#include "tcop/dest.h"

/*
 * A struct to hold COPY options, in a parsed form. All of these are related
 * to formatting, except for 'freeze', which doesn't really belong here, but
 * it's expedient to parse it along with all the other options.
 */
typedef struct CopyFormatOptions
{
	/* parameters from the COPY command */
	int			file_encoding;	/* file or remote side's character encoding,
								 * -1 if not specified */
	bool		binary;			/* binary format? */
	bool		freeze;			/* freeze rows on loading? */
	bool		csv_mode;		/* Comma Separated Value format? */
	bool		header_line;	/* CSV header line? */
	char	   *null_print;		/* NULL marker string (server encoding!) */
	int			null_print_len; /* length of same */
	char	   *null_print_client;	/* same converted to file encoding */
	char	   *delim;			/* column delimiter (must be 1 byte) */
	char	   *quote;			/* CSV quote char (must be 1 byte) */
	char	   *escape;			/* CSV escape char (must be 1 byte) */
	List	   *force_quote;	/* list of column names */
	bool		force_quote_all;	/* FORCE_QUOTE *? */
	bool	   *force_quote_flags;	/* per-column CSV FQ flags */
	List	   *force_notnull;	/* list of column names */
	bool	   *force_notnull_flags;	/* per-column CSV FNN flags */
	List	   *force_null;		/* list of column
... (truncated)

/*
 * Process the statement option list for COPY.
 *
 * Scan the options list (a list of DefElem) and transpose the information
 * into *opts_out, applying appropriate error checking.
 *
 * If 'opts_out' is not NULL, it is assumed to be filled with zeroes initially.
 *
 * This is exported so that external users of the COPY API can sanity-check
 * a list of options.  In that usage, 'opts_out' can be passed as NULL and
 * the collected data is just leaked until CurrentMemoryContext is reset.
 *
 * Note that additional checking, such as whether column names listed in FORCE
 * QUOTE actually exist, has to be applied later.  This just checks for
 * self-consistency of the options list.
 */
void

				   CopyFormatOptions *opts_out,
				   bool is_from,
				   List *options)
{

	bool		freeze_specified = false;
	bool		header_specified = false;
	ListCell   *option;

		{

222-assistanttool_useBash
223-usertool_resultBash
 * NOTE: force_not_null option are not applied to the returned fields.
 */
bool
NextCopyFromRawFields(CopyFromState cstate, char ***fields, int *nfields)
{
	int			fldct;
	bool		done;

	/* only available for text or csv input */
	Assert(!cstate->opts.binary);

	/* on input just throw the header line away */
	if (cstate->cur_lineno == 0 && cstate->opts.header_line)
	{
		cstate->cur_lineno++;
		if (CopyReadLine(cstate))
			return false;		/* done */
	}

	cstate->cur_lineno++;

	/* Actually read the line into memory here */
	done = CopyReadLine(cstate);

	/*
	 * EOF at start of line means we're done.  If we see EOF after some
	 * characters, we act as though it was newline followed by EOF, ie,
	 * process the line and then exit loop on next iteration.
	 */
	if (done && cstate->line_buf.len == 0)
		return false;

	/* Parse the line into de-escaped field values */
	if (cstate->opts.csv_mode)
		fldct = CopyReadAttributesCSV(cstate);
	else
		fldct = CopyReadAttributesText(cstate);

	*fields = cstate->raw_fields;
	*nfields = fldct;
	return true;
}

/*
 * Read next tuple from file for COPY FROM. Return false if no more tuples.
 *
 * 'econtext' is used to evaluate default expression for each columns not
 * read from the file. It can be NULL when no default values are used, i.e.
 * when all columns are read from the file.
 *
 * 'values' and 'nulls' arrays must be the same length as columns of the

 * An internal temporary buffer is returned via 'fields'. It is valid until
 * the next call of the function. Since the function returns all raw fields
 * in the input file, 'nfields' could be different from the number of columns
 * in the relation.
 *
 * NOTE: force_not_null option are not applied to the returned fields.
 */
bool
NextCopyFromRawFields(CopyFromState cstate, char ***fields, int *nfields)
{
	int			fldct;
	bool		done;

	/* only available for text or csv input */
	Assert(!cstate->opts.binary);

	/* on input just throw the header line away */
	if (cstate->cur_lineno == 0 && cstate->opts.header_line)
	{
		cstate->cur_lineno++;
		if (CopyReadLine(cstate))
			return false;		/* done */

{
	int			fldct;
	bool		done;

	/* only available for text or csv input */
	Assert(!cstate->opts.binary);

	/* on input check that the header line is correct if needed */
	if (cstate->cur_lineno == 0 && cstate->opts.header_line)
	{
		ListCell   *cur;
		TupleDesc	tupDesc;

		{
			int			fldnum;

			if (cstate->opts.csv_mode)
				fldct = CopyReadAttributesCSV(cstate);
			else
				fldct = CopyReadAttributesText(cstate);

			if (fldct != list_length(cstate->attnumlist))
				ereport(ERROR,
						(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),
						 errmsg("wrong number of fields in header line: got %d, expected %d",
								fldct, list_length(cstate->attnumlist))));

			{
				int			attnum = lfirst_int(cur);
				char	   *colName;
				Form_pg_attribute attr = TupleDescAttr(tupDesc, attnum - 1);

				Assert(fldnum < cstate->max_fields);

				colName = cstate->raw_fields[fldnum++];
				if (colName == NULL)
					ereport(ERROR,
							(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),
							 errmsg("column name mismatch in header line field %d: got null value (\"%s\"), expected \"%s\"",
									fldnum, cstate->opts.null_print, NameStr(attr->attname))));

				if (namestrcmp(&attr->attname, colName) != 0)
				{
					ereport(ERROR,
							(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),
							 errmsg("column name mismatch in header line field %d: got \"%s\", expected \"%s\"",
									fldnum, colName, NameStr(attr->attname))));
				}
			}
		}

		if (done)
			return false;
	}

	cstate->cur_lineno++;

	/* Actually read the line into memory here */
	done = CopyReadLine(cstate);

329-usertext-
This session is being continued from a previous conversation that ran out of context. The summary below covers the earlier portion of the conversation.

Summary:
1. Primary Request and Intent:
   The task is to implement `COPY FROM CSV WITH HEADER MATCH` for PostgreSQL. This feature validates the CSV file's header row column names match the target table's column names (in order and spelling). Currently `COPY ... WITH (HEADER)` simply skips the first row; `HEADER MATCH` should verify it matches.

   Requirements:
   - Extend COPY grammar (`src/backend/parser/gram.y`): Add MATCH as a valid keyword after HEADER in COPY options
   - Update COPY option processing (`src/backend/commands/copy.c`): Parse HEADER MATCH option, set a flag using CopyHeaderChoice enum (OFF, ON, MATCH)
   - Implement header validation in `src/backend/commands/copyfromparse.c`: Compare CSV header columns to target table column names (case-insensitive)
   - Add regression tests in `src/test/regress/sql/copy.sql` with both matching/mismatching test cases

2. Key Technical Concepts:
   - PostgreSQL COPY command implementation (copy.c, copyfromparse.c)
   - `CopyHeaderChoice` enum: `COPY_HEADER_FALSE=0`, `COPY_HEADER_TRUE`, `COPY_HEADER_MATCH`
   - `CopyFormatOptions` struct: holds COPY options including `header_line` field
   - `defGetCopyHeaderChoice()` function: extracts CopyHeaderChoice from DefElem, accepts "true"/"false"/"on"/"off"/"match"
   - `NextCopyFromRawFields()` function in copyfromparse.c: reads raw fields with header validation
   - `namestrcmp()` for case-insensitive column name comparison (from `utils/builtins.h`)
   - PostgreSQL grammar using `copy_generic_opt_list` (new-style parenthesized options) for `(header match)` syntax
   - MATCH is already an UNRESERVED_KEYWORD in kwlist.h, acc
... (truncated)

In the \"TO\" case\n47:  * we also support copying the output of an arbitrary SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE\n48:  * or DELETE query.\n49:  *\n50:  * If <pipe> is false, transfer is between the table and the file named\n51:  * <filename>.  Otherwise, transfer is between the table and our regular\n52:  * input/output stream. \t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   \"pg_execute_server_program\"),\n87: \t\t\t\t\t\t errhint(\"Anyone can COPY to stdout or from stdin. \"\n88: \t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t \"psql's \\\\copy command also works for anyone.\")));\n89: \t\t}\n90: \t\telse\n91: \t\t{\n92: \t\t\tif (is_from && !has_privs_of_role(GetUserId(), ROLE_PG_READ_SERVER_FILES))\n93: \t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n94: enabled for this, then just fall through to the\n\t\t * normal non-filtering relation handling.\n\t\t */\n\t\tif (check_enable_rls(rte->relid, InvalidOid, false) == RLS_ENABLED)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tSelectStmt *select;\n\t\t\tColumnRef  *cr;\n\t\t\tResTarget  *target;\n\t\t\tRangeVar   *from;\n\t\t\tList\t   *targetList = NIL;\n\n\t\t\tif (is_from)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY FROM not supported with row-level security\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errhint(\"Use INSERT statements instead.\")));\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Build target list\n\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t * If no columns are specified in the attribute list of the COPY\n\t\t\t * command, then the target list is 'all' columns. Therefore, '*'\n\t\t\t * should be used as the target list for the resulting SELECT\n\t\t\t * statement.\n\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t * In the case that columns are specified in the attribute list,\n\t\t\t * create a ColumnRef and ResTarget for each column and add them\n\t\t\t * to the target list for the resulting SELECT statement.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (!stmt->attlist)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tcr = makeNode(ColumnRef);\n\t\t\t\tcr->fields = list_make1(makeNode(A_Star));\n\t\t\t\tcr->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\ttarget = makeNode(ResTarget);\n\t\t\t\ttarget->name = NULL;\n\t\t\t\ttarget->indirection = NIL;\n\t\t\t\ttarget->val = (Node *) cr;\n\t\t\t\ttarget->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\ttargetList = list_make1(target);\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tListCell   *lc;\n\n\t\t\t\tforeach(lc, stmt->attlist)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t\t * Build the ColumnRef for each column.  The ColumnRef\n\t\t\t\t\t * 'fields' property is a String 'Value' node (see\n\t\t\t\t\t * nodes/value.h) that corresponds to the column name\n\t\t\t\t\t * respectively.\n\t\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\t\tcr = makeNode(ColumnRef);\n\t\t\t\t\tcr->fields = list_make1(lfirst(lc));\n\t\t\t\t\tcr->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\t\t/* Build the ResTarget and add the ColumnRef to it. */\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget = makeNode(ResTarget);\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->name = NULL;\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->indirection = NIL;\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->val = (Node *) cr;\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\t\t/* Add each column to the SELECT statement's target list */\n\t\t\t\t\ttargetList = lappend(targetList, target);\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Build RangeVar for from clause, fully qualified based on the\n\t\t\t * relation which we have opened and locked.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tfrom = makeRangeVar(get_namespace_name(RelationGetNamespace(rel)),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tpstrdup(RelationGetRelationName(rel)),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t-1);\n\n\t\t\t/* Build query */\n\t\t\tselect = makeNode(SelectStmt);\n\t\t\tselect->targetList = targetList;\n\t\t\tselect->fromClause = list_make1(from);\n\n\t\t\tquery = makeNode(RawStmt);\n\t\t\tquery->stmt = (Node *) select;\n\t\t\tquery->stmt_location = stmt_location;\n\t\t\tquery->stmt_len = stmt_len;\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Close the relation for now, but keep the lock on it to prevent\n\t\t\t * changes between now and when we start the query-based COPY.\n\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t * We'll reopen it later as part of the query-based COPY.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\ttable_close(rel, NoLock);\n\t\t\trel = NULL;\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\telse\n\t{\n\t\tAssert(stmt->query);\n\n\t\tquery = makeNode(RawStmt);\n\t\tquery->stmt = stmt->query;\n\t\tquery->stmt_location = stmt_location;\n\t\tquery->stmt_len = stmt_len;\n\n\t\trelid = InvalidOid;\n\t\trel = NULL;\n\t}\n\n\tif (is_from)\n\t{\n\t\tCopyFromState cstate;\n\n\t\tAssert(rel);\n\n\t\t/* check read-only transaction and parallel mode */\n\t\tif (XactReadOnly && !rel->rd_islocaltemp)\n\t\t\tPreventCommandIfReadOnly(\"COPY FROM\");\n\n\t\tcstate = BeginCopyFrom(pstate, rel, whereClause,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   stmt->filename, stmt->is_program,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   NULL, stmt->attlist, stmt->options);\n\t\t*processed = CopyFrom(cstate);\t/* copy from file to database */\n\t\tEndCopyFrom(cstate);\n\t}\n\telse\n\t{\n\t\tCopyToState cstate;\n\n\t\tcstate = BeginCopyTo(pstate, rel, query, relid,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t stmt->filename, stmt->is_program,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t stmt->attlist, stmt->options);\n\t\t*processed = DoCopyTo(cstate);\t/* copy from database to file */\n\t\tEndCopyTo(cstate);\n\t}\n\n\tif (rel != NULL)\n\t\ttable_close(rel, NoLock);\n}\n\n/*\n * Process the statement option list for COPY.\n *\n * Scan the options list (a list of DefElem) and transpose the information\n * into *opts_out, applying appropriate error checking.\n *\n * If 'opts_out' is not NULL, it is assumed to be filled with zeroes initially.\n *\n * This is exported so that external users of the COPY API can sanity-check\n * a list of options.  In that usage, 'opts_out' can be passed as NULL and\n * the collected data is just leaked until CurrentMemoryContext is reset.\n *\n * Note that additional checking, such as whether column names listed in FORCE\n * QUOTE actually exist, has to be applied later.  This just checks for\n * self-consistency of the options list.\n */\nvoid\nProcessCopyOptions(ParseState *pstate,\n\t\t\t\t   CopyFormatOptions *opts_out,\n\t\t\t\t   bool is_from,\n\t\t\t\t   List *options)\n{\n\tbool\t\tformat_specified = false;\n\tbool\t\tfreeze_specified = false;\n\tbool\t\theader_specified = false;\n\tListCell   *option;\n\n\t/* Support external use for option sanity checking */\n\tif (opts_out == NULL)\n\t\topts_out = (CopyFormatOptions *) palloc0(sizeof(CopyFormatOptions));\n\n\topts_out->file_encoding = -1;\n\n\t/* Extract options from the statement node tree */\n\tforeach(option, options)\n\t{\n\t\tDefElem    *defel = lfirst_node(DefElem, option);\n\n\t\tif (strcmp(defel->defname, \"format\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tchar\t   *fmt = defGetString(defel);\n\n\t\t\tif (format_specified)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t\tformat_specified = true;\n\t\t\tif (strcmp(fmt, \"text\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t /* default format */ ;\n\t\t\telse if (strcmp(fmt, \"csv\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\topts_out->csv_mode = true;\n\t\t\telse if (strcmp(fmt, \"binary\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\topts_out->binary = true;\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY format \\\"%s\\\" not recognized\", fmt),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"freeze\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (freeze_specified)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t\tfreeze_specified = true;\n\t\t\topts_out->freeze = defGetBoolean(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"delimiter\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->delim)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t\topts_out->delim = defGetString(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"null\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->null_print)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t\topts_out->null_print = defGetString(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"header\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (header_specified)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t\theader_specified = true;\n\t\t\topts_out->header_line = defGetBoolean(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"quote\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->quote)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t\topts_out->quote = defGetString(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"escape\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->escape)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t\topts_out->escape = defGetString(defel);\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"force_quote\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->force_quote || opts_out->force_quote_all)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t\tif (defel->arg && IsA(defel->arg, A_Star))\n\t\t\t\topts_out->force_quote_all = true;\n\t\t\telse if (defel->arg && IsA(defel->arg, List))\n\t\t\t\topts_out->force_quote = castNode(List, defel->arg);\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"argument to option \\\"%s\\\" must be a list of column names\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefel->defname),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"force_not_null\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->force_notnull)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t\tif (defel->arg && IsA(defel->arg, List))\n\t\t\t\topts_out->force_notnull = castNode(List, defel->arg);\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"argument to option \\\"%s\\\" must be a list of column names\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefel->defname),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"force_null\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->force_null)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\")));\n\t\t\tif (defel->arg && IsA(defel->arg, List))\n\t\t\t\topts_out->force_null = castNode(List, defel->arg);\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"argument to option \\\"%s\\\" must be a list of column names\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefel->defname),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"convert_selectively\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Undocumented, not-accessible-from-SQL option: convert only the\n\t\t\t * named columns to binary form, storing the rest as NULLs. It's\n\t\t\t * allowed for the column list to be NIL.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->convert_selectively)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t\topts_out->convert_selectively = true;\n\t\t\tif (defel->arg == NULL || IsA(defel->arg, List))\n\t\t\t\topts_out->convert_select = castNode(List, defel->arg);\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"argument to option \\\"%s\\\" must be a list of column names\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefel->defname),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse if (strcmp(defel->defname, \"encoding\") == 0)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->file_encoding >= 0)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"conflicting or redundant options\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t\topts_out->file_encoding = pg_char_to_encoding(defGetString(defel));\n\t\t\tif (opts_out->file_encoding < 0)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"argument to option \\\"%s\\\" must be a valid encoding name\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefel->defname),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse\n\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"option \\\"%s\\\" not recognized\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdefel->defname),\n\t\t\t\t\t parser_errposition(pstate, defel->location)));\n\t}\n\n\t/*\n\t * Check for incompatible options (must do these two before inserting\n\t * defaults)\n\t */\n\tif (opts_out->binary && opts_out->delim)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"cannot specify DELIMITER in BINARY mode\")));\n\n\tif (opts_out->binary && opts_out->null_print)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"cannot specify NULL in BINARY mode\")));\n\n\t/* Set defaults for omitted options */\n\tif (!opts_out->delim)\n\t\topts_out->delim = opts_out->csv_mode ? \",\" : \"\\t\";\n\n\tif (!opts_out->null_print)\n\t\topts_out->null_print = opts_out->csv_mode ? \"\" : \"\\\\N\";\n\topts_out->null_print_len = strlen(opts_out->null_print);\n\n\tif (opts_out->csv_mode)\n\t{\n\t\tif (!opts_out->quote)\n\t\t\topts_out->quote = \"\\\"\";\n\t\tif (!opts_out->escape)\n\t\t\topts_out->escape = opts_out->quote;\n\t}\n\n\t/* Only single-byte delimiter strings are supported. */\n\tif (strlen(opts_out->delim) != 1)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY delimiter must be a single one-byte character\")));\n\n\t/* Disallow end-of-line characters */\n\tif (strchr(opts_out->delim, '\\r') != NULL ||\n\t\tstrchr(opts_out->delim, '\\n') != NULL)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY delimiter cannot be newline or carriage return\")));\n\n\tif (strchr(opts_out->null_print, '\\r') != NULL ||\n\t\tstrchr(opts_out->null_print, '\\n') != NULL)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY null representation cannot use newline or carriage return\")));\n\n\t/*\n\t * Disallow unsafe delimiter characters in non-CSV mode.  We can't allow\n\t * backslash because it would be ambiguous.  We can't allow the other\n\t * cases because data characters matching the delimiter must be\n\t * backslashed, and certain backslash combinations are interpreted\n\t * non-literally by COPY IN.  Disallowing all lower case ASCII letters is\n\t * more than strictly necessary, but seems best for consistency and\n\t * future-proofing.  Likewise we disallow all digits though only octal\n\t * digits are actually dangerous.\n\t */\n\tif (!opts_out->csv_mode &&\n\t\tstrchr(\"\\\\.abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789\",\n\t\t\t   opts_out->delim[0]) != NULL)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY delimiter cannot be \\\"%s\\\"\", opts_out->delim)));\n\n\t/* Check header */\n\tif (!opts_out->csv_mode && opts_out->header_line)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY HEADER available only in CSV mode\")));\n\n\t/* Check quote */\n\tif (!opts_out->csv_mode && opts_out->quote != NULL)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY quote available only in CSV mode\")));\n\n\tif (opts_out->csv_mode && strlen(opts_out->quote) != 1)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY quote must be a single one-byte character\")));\n\n\tif (opts_out->csv_mode && opts_out->delim[0] == opts_out->quote[0])\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INVALID_PARAMETER_VALUE),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY delimiter and quote must be different\")));\n\n\t/* Check escape */\n\tif (!opts_out->csv_mode && opts_out->escape != NULL)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY escape available only in CSV mode\")));\n\n\tif (opts_out->csv_mode && strlen(opts_out->escape) != 1)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY escape must be a single one-byte character\")));\n\n\t/* Check force_quote */\n\tif (!opts_out->csv_mode && (opts_out->force_quote || opts_out->force_quote_all))\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY force quote available only in CSV mode\")));\n\tif ((opts_out->force_quote || opts_out->force_quote_all) && is_from)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY force quote only available using COPY TO\")));\n\n\t/* Check force_notnull */\n\tif (!opts_out->csv_mode && opts_out->force_notnull != NIL)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY force not null available only in CSV mode\")));\n\tif (opts_out->force_notnull != NIL && !is_from)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY force not null only available using COPY FROM\")));\n\n\t/* Check force_null */\n\tif (!opts_out->csv_mode && opts_out->force_null != NIL)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY force null available only in CSV mode\")));\n\n\tif (opts_out->force_null != NIL && !is_from)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY force null only available using COPY FROM\")));\n\n\t/* Don't allow the delimiter to appear in the null string. */\n\tif (strchr(opts_out->null_print, opts_out->delim[0]) != NULL)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY delimiter must not appear in the NULL specification\")));\n\n\t/* Don't allow the CSV quote char to appear in the null string. */\n\tif (opts_out->csv_mode &&\n\t\tstrchr(opts_out->null_print, opts_out->quote[0]) != NULL)\n\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"CSV quote character must not appear in the NULL specification\")));\n}\n\n/*\n * CopyGetAttnums - build But this way it's at\n * least ensured that whatever we copy out can be copied back in.\n *\n * rel can be NULL ... it's only used for error reports.\n */\nList *\nCopyGetAttnums(TupleDesc tupDesc, Relation rel, List *attnamelist)\n{\n\tList\t   *attnums = NIL;\n\n\tif (attnamelist == NIL)\n\t{\n\t\t/* Generate default column list */\n\t\tint\t\t\tattr_count = tupDesc->natts;\n\t\tint\t\t\ti;\n\n\t\tfor (i = 0; In the \"TO\" case\n * we also support copying the output of an arbitrary SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE\n * or DELETE query.\n *\n * If <pipe> is false, transfer is between the table and the file named\n * <filename>.  Otherwise, transfer is between the table and our regular\n * input/output stream. The latter could be either stdin/stdout or a\n * socket, depending on whether we're running under Postmaster control.\n *\n * Do not allow a Postgres user without the 'pg_read_server_files' or\n * This is like\n * defGetBoolean() but also accepts the special value \"match\".\n */\nstatic CopyHeaderChoice\ndefGetCopyHeaderChoice(DefElem *def, bool is_from)\n{\n\t/*\n\t * If no parameter given, anyone.\")));\n\t\t}\n\t\telse\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tif (is_from && !is_member_of_role(GetUserId(), ROLE_PG_READ_SERVER_FILES))\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_INSUFFICIENT_PRIVILEGE),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"must be superuser or a member of the pg_read_server_files role to COPY pg_write_server_files role to COPY to a file\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errhint(\"Anyone can COPY to stdout or from stdin. \"\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t \"psql's \\\\copy command also works for RowExclusiveLock : AccessShareLock;\n\t\tParseNamespaceItem *nsitem;\n\t\tRangeTblEntry *rte;\n\t\tTupleDesc\ttupDesc;\n\t\tList\t   *attnums;\n\t\tListCell   *cur;\n\n\t\tAssert(!stmt->query);\n\n\t\t/* Open and lock the relation, using the appropriate lock type. */\n\t\trel = table_openrv(stmt->relation, lockmode);\n\n\t\trelid = RelationGetRelid(rel);\n\n\t\tnsitem = addRangeTableEntryForRelation(pstate, rel, lockmode,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   NULL, false, false);\n\t\trte = nsitem->p_rte;\n\t\trte->requiredPerms = (is_from ? ACL_INSERT : ACL_SELECT);\n\n\t\tif (stmt->whereClause)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\t/* add nsitem to query namespace */\n\t\t\taddNSItemToQuery(pstate, nsitem, false, true, true);\n\n\t\t\t/* Transform the raw expression tree */\n\t\t\twhereClause = transformExpr(pstate, stmt->whereClause, EXPR_KIND_COPY_WHERE);\n\n\t\t\t/* Make sure it yields a boolean result. */\n\t\t\twhereClause = coerce_to_boolean(pstate, whereClause, \"WHERE\");\n\n\t\t\t/* we have to fix its collations too */\n\t\t\tassign_expr_collations(pstate, whereClause);\n\n\t\t\twhereClause = eval_const_expressions(NULL, whereClause);\n\n\t\t\twhereClause = (Node *) canonicalize_qual((Expr *) whereClause, false);\n\t\t\twhereClause = (Node *) make_ands_implicit((Expr *) whereClause);\n\t\t}\n\n\t\ttupDesc = RelationGetDescr(rel);\n\t\tattnums = CopyGetAttnums(tupDesc, rel, stmt->attlist);\n\t\tforeach(cur, attnums)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tint\t\t\tattno = lfirst_int(cur) -\n\t\t\tFirstLowInvalidHeapAttributeNumber;\n\n\t\t\tif (is_from)\n\t\t\t\trte->insertedCols = bms_add_member(rte->insertedCols, attno);\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t\trte->selectedCols = bms_add_member(rte->selectedCols, attno);\n\t\t}\n\t\tExecCheckRTPerms(pstate->p_rtable, true);\n\n\t\t/*\n\t\t * Permission check for row security policies.\n\t\t *\n\t\t * check_enable_rls will ereport(ERROR) if the user has requested\n\t\t * something invalid and will otherwise indicate if we should enable\n\t\t * RLS (returns RLS_ENABLED) or not for this COPY statement.\n\t\t *\n\t\t * If the relation has a row security policy and we are to apply it\n\t\t * then perform a \"query\" copy and allow the normal query processing\n\t\t * to handle the policies.\n\t\t *\n\t\t * If RLS is not enabled for this, then just fall through to the\n\t\t * normal non-filtering relation handling.\n\t\t */\n\t\tif (check_enable_rls(rte->relid, InvalidOid, false) == RLS_ENABLED)\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tSelectStmt *select;\n\t\t\tColumnRef  *cr;\n\t\t\tResTarget  *target;\n\t\t\tRangeVar   *from;\n\t\t\tList\t   *targetList = NIL;\n\n\t\t\tif (is_from)\n\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"COPY FROM not supported with row-level security\"),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t errhint(\"Use INSERT statements instead.\")));\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Build target list\n\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t * If no columns are specified in the attribute list of the COPY\n\t\t\t * command, then the target list is 'all' columns. Therefore, '*'\n\t\t\t * should be used as the target list for the resulting SELECT\n\t\t\t * statement.\n\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t * In the case that columns are specified in the attribute list,\n\t\t\t * create a ColumnRef and ResTarget for each column and add them\n\t\t\t * to the target list for the resulting SELECT statement.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tif (!stmt->attlist)\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tcr = makeNode(ColumnRef);\n\t\t\t\tcr->fields = list_make1(makeNode(A_Star));\n\t\t\t\tcr->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\ttarget = makeNode(ResTarget);\n\t\t\t\ttarget->name = NULL;\n\t\t\t\ttarget->indirection = NIL;\n\t\t\t\ttarget->val = (Node *) cr;\n\t\t\t\ttarget->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\ttargetList = list_make1(target);\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\telse\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tListCell   *lc;\n\n\t\t\t\tforeach(lc, stmt->attlist)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t\t * Build the ColumnRef for each column.  The ColumnRef\n\t\t\t\t\t * 'fields' property is a String 'Value' node (see\n\t\t\t\t\t * nodes/value.h) that corresponds to the column name\n\t\t\t\t\t * respectively.\n\t\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\t\tcr = makeNode(ColumnRef);\n\t\t\t\t\tcr->fields = list_make1(lfirst(lc));\n\t\t\t\t\tcr->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\t\t/* Build the ResTarget and add the ColumnRef to it. */\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget = makeNode(ResTarget);\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->name = NULL;\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->indirection = NIL;\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->val = (Node *) cr;\n\t\t\t\t\ttarget->location = -1;\n\n\t\t\t\t\t/* Add each column to the SELECT statement's target list */\n\t\t\t\t\ttargetList = lappend(targetList, target);\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Build RangeVar for from clause, fully qualified based on the\n\t\t\t * relation which we have opened and locked.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\tfrom = makeRangeVar(get_namespace_name(RelationGetNamespace(rel)),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tpstrdup(RelationGetRelationName(rel)),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t-1);\n\n\t\t\t/* Build query */\n\t\t\tselect = makeNode(SelectStmt);\n\t\t\tselect->targetList = targetList;\n\t\t\tselect->fromClause = list_make1(from);\n\n\t\t\tquery = makeNode(RawStmt);\n\t\t\tquery->stmt = (Node *) select;\n\t\t\tquery->stmt_location = stmt_location;\n\t\t\tquery->stmt_len = stmt_len;\n\n\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t * Close the relation for now, but keep the lock on it to prevent\n\t\t\t * changes between now and when we start the query-based COPY.\n\t\t\t *\n\t\t\t * We'll reopen it later as part of the query-based COPY.\n\t\t\t */\n\t\t\ttable_close(rel, NoLock);\n\t\t\trel = NULL;\n\t\t}\n\t}\n\telse\n\t{\n\t\tAssert(stmt->query);\n\n\t\tquery = makeNode(RawStmt);\n\t\tquery->stmt = stmt->query;\n\t\tquery->stmt_location = stmt_location;\n\t\tquery->stmt_len = stmt_len;\n\n\t\trelid = InvalidOid;\n\t\trel = NULL;\n\t}\n\n\tif (is_from)\n\t{\n\t\tCopyFromState cstate;\n\n\t\tAssert(rel);\n\n\t\t/* check read-only transaction and parallel mode */\n\t\tif (XactReadOnly && !rel->rd_islocaltemp)\n\t\t\tPreventCommandIfReadOnly(\"COPY FROM\");\n\n\t\tcstate = BeginCopyFrom(pstate, rel, whereClause,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   stmt->filename, stmt->is_program,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t   NULL, stmt->attlist, stmt->options);\n\t\t*processed = CopyFrom(cstate);\t/* copy from file to database */\n\t\tEndCopyFrom(cstate);\n\t}\n\telse\n\t{\n\t\tCopyToState cstate;\n\n\t\tcstate = BeginCopyTo(pstate, rel, query, relid,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t stmt->filename, stmt->is_program,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t stmt->attlist, stmt->options);\n\t\t*processed = DoCopyTo(cstate);\t/* copy from database to file */\n\t\tEndCopyTo(cstate);\n\t}\n\n\tif (rel != NULL)\n\t\ttable_close(rel, NoLock);\n}\n\n/*\n * Extract a CopyHeaderChoice value from a DefElem.  This is like\n * defGetBoolean() but also accepts the special value \"match\".\n */\nstatic CopyHeaderChoice\ndefGetCopyHeaderChoice(DefElem *def, bool is_from)\n{\n\t/*\n\t * If no parameter given, assume \"true\" is meant.\n\t */\n\tif (def->arg == NULL)\n\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_TRUE;\n\n\t/*\n\t * Allow 0, 1, \"true\", \"false\", \"on\", \"off\", or \"match\".\n\t */\n\tswitch (nodeTag(def->arg))\n\t{\n\t\tcase T_Integer:\n\t\t\tswitch (intVal(def->arg))\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tcase 0:\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_FALSE;\n\t\t\t\tcase 1:\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_TRUE;\n\t\t\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t\t\t/* otherwise, error out below */\n\t\t\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t\tdefault:\n\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\tchar\t   *sval = defGetString(def);\n\n\t\t\t\t/*\n\t\t\t\t * The set of strings accepted here should match up with the\n\t\t\t\t * grammar's opt_boolean_or_string production.\n\t\t\t\t */\n\t\t\t\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"true\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_TRUE;\n\t\t\t\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"false\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_FALSE;\n\t\t\t\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"on\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_TRUE;\n\t\t\t\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"off\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_FALSE;\n\t\t\t\tif (pg_strcasecmp(sval, \"match\") == 0)\n\t\t\t\t{\n\t\t\t\t\tif (!is_from)\n\t\t\t\t\t\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_FEATURE_NOT_SUPPORTED),\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t errmsg(\"cannot use \\\"%s\\\" with HEADER in COPY TO\",\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tsval)));\n\t\t\t\t\treturn COPY_HEADER_MATCH;\n\t\t\t\t}\n\t\t\t}\n\t\t\tbreak;\n\t}\n\tereport(ERROR,\n\t\t\t(errcode(ERRCODE_SYNTAX_ERROR),\n\t\t\t errmsg(\"%s requires a Boolean value or \\\"match\\\"\",\n\t\t\t\t\tdef->defname)));\n\treturn COPY_HEADER_FALSE;\t/* keep compiler quiet */\n}\n\n/*\n * Process the statement option list for COPY.\n *\n * Scan the options In that usage, 'opts_out' can be passed as NULL and\n * the collected data is just leaked until CurrentMemoryContext is reset.\n *\n * Note that additional checking, such as whether column names listed in FORCE\n * QUOTE actually exist, has to be applied later. checking */\n\tif (opts_out == NULL)\n\t\topts_out = (CopyFormatOptions *) palloc0(sizeof(CopyFormatOptions));\n\n\topts_out->file_encoding = -1;\n\n\t/* Extract options from the statement node tree /*-------------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 * copy.h
 *	  Definitions for using the POSTGRES copy command.
 *
 *
 * Portions Copyright (c) 1996-2022, PostgreSQL Global Development Group
 * Portions Copyright (c) 1994, Regents of the University of California
 *
 * src/include/commands/copy.h
 *
 *-------------------------------------------------------------------------
 */
#ifndef COPY_H
#define COPY_H

#include "nodes/execnodes.h"
#include "nodes/parsenodes.h"
#include "parser/parse_node.h"
#include "tcop/dest.h"

/*
 * Represents whether a header line should be present, and whether it must
 * match the actual names (which implies "true").
 */
typedef enum CopyHeaderChoice
{
	COPY_HEADER_FALSE = 0,
	COPY_HEADER_TRUE,
	COPY_HEADER_MATCH,
} CopyHeaderChoice;

/*
 * A struct to hold COPY options, in a parsed form. All of these are related
 * to formatting, except for 'freeze', which doesn't really belong here, but
 * it's expedient to parse it along with all the other options.
 */
typedef struct CopyFormatOptions
{
	/* parameters from the COPY command */
	int			file_encoding;	/* file or remote side's character encoding,
								 * -1 if not specified */
	bool		binary;			/* binary format? */
	bool		freeze;			/* freeze rows on loading? */
	bool		csv_mode;		/* Comma Separated Value format? */
	CopyHeaderChoice header_line;	/* header line? */
	char	   *null_print;		/* NULL marker string (server encoding!) */
	int			null_print_len; /* length of same */
	char	   *null_print_client;	/* same converted to file encoding */
	char	   *delim;			/* column delimiter (must be 1 byte) */
	char	   *quote;			/* CSV quote char (must be 1 byte) */
	char	   *escape;			/* CSV escape char (must be 1 byte) */
	List	   *force_quote;	/* list of column names */
	bo

/*
 *	 DoCopy executes the SQL COPY statement
 *
 * Either unload or reload contents of table <relation>, depending on <from>.
 * (<from> = true means we are inserting into the table.)  In the "TO" case
 * we also support copying the output of an arbitrary SELECT, INSERT, UPDATE
 * or DELETE query.
 *
 * If <pipe> is false, transfer is between the table and the file named
 * <filename>.  Otherwise, transfer is between the table and our regular
 * input/output stream. The latter could be either stdin/stdout or a
 * socket, depending on whether we're running under Postmaster control.
 *
 * Do not allow a Postgres user without the 'pg_read_server_files' or

67. $ python3 << 'EOF'
with open('/tmp/postgres-src/src/backend/commands/copyfromparse.c', 'r') as f:
    content = f.read()

old_code = '''	/* on input just throw the header line away */
	if (cstate->cur_lineno == 0 && cstate->opts.header_line)
	{
		cstate->cur_lineno++;
		if (CopyReadLine(cstate))
			return false;		/* done */
	}'''

new_code = '''	/* on input check that the header line is correct if needed */
	if (cstate->cur_lineno == 0 && cstate->opts.header_line)
	{
		ListCell   *cur;
		TupleDesc	tupDesc;

		tupDesc = RelationGetDescr(cstate->rel);

		cstate->cur_lineno++;
		done = CopyReadLine(cstate);

		if (cstate->opts.header_line == COPY_HEADER_MATCH)
		{
			int			fldnum;

			if (cstate->opts.csv_mode)
				fldct = CopyReadAttributesCSV(cstate);
			else
				fldct = CopyReadAttributesText(cstate);

			if (fldct != list_length(cstate->attnumlist))
				ereport(ERROR,
						(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),
						 errmsg("wrong number of fields in header line: got %d, expected %d",
								fldct, list_length(cstate->attnumlist))));

			fldnum = 0;
			foreach(cur, cstate->attnumlist)
			{
				int			attnum = lfirst_int(cur);
				char	   *colName;
				Form_pg_attribute attr = TupleDescAttr(tupDesc, attnum - 1);

				Assert(fldnum < cstate->max_fields);

				colName = cstate->raw_fields[fldnum++];
				if (colName == NULL)
					ereport(ERROR,
							(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),
							 errmsg("column name mismatch in header line field %d: got null value (\\"%s\\"), expected \\"%s\\"",
									fldnum, cstate->opts.null_print, NameStr(attr->attname))));

				if (namestrcmp(&attr->attname, colName) != 0)
				{
					ereport(ERROR,
							(errcode(ERRCODE_BAD_COPY_FILE_FORMAT),
							 errmsg("column name mismatch in header line field %d: got \\"%s\\", expected \\"%s\\"",
									fldnum, colName, NameStr(attr->attname))));
				}
			}
		}

		if (done)
			return false;
	}'''

if old_code in content:
    new_content = content.replace(old_code, new_code, 1)
    with open('/workspace/src/backend/commands/copyfromparse.c', 'w') as f:
        f.write(new_content)
    print("Success: wrote modified copyfromparse.c")
else:
    print("ERROR: old_code not found!")
    # Find nearby context
    idx = content.find("on input just throw")
    if idx >= 0:
        print(f"Found at index {idx}")
        print(repr(content[idx:idx+200]))
EOF
